Визуализация должна:\n*   Строиться **максимально быстро** после загрузки/выбора аудиофайла, до начала какого-либо воспроизведения.\n*   Быть **полностью отвязана** от процесса воспроизведения и состояния окна браузера.\n*   Позволять мгновенно отображать визуализацию для любой части трека при его прокрутке (скраббинге).\n*   Поддерживать оба режима: \"живой\" рендеринг с микрофона и \"предварительный\" для загруженных файлов.\n\n**Технические требования/предложения по реализации:**\n\n1.  **Offline Audio Context и декодирование аудиоданных:**\n    *   Использовать `OfflineAudioContext` для обработки аудио без его вывода на динамики.\n    *   Декодировать весь загруженный аудиофайл в `ArrayBuffer` с помощью `AudioContext.decodeAudioData()`.\n    *   Полученный `AudioBuffer` содержит все PCM-данные (каналы, сэмплы), доступные для синхронного анализа.\n\n2.  **Предварительный анализ и даунсэмплинг:**\n    *   Разработать функцию-анализатор, которая проходит по всему `AudioBuffer` (или его части для очень длинных файлов с шагом).\n    *   **Даунсэмплинг данных:** Не нужно анализировать каждый сэмпл (их могут быть миллионы). Для визуализации на канвасе шириной 1000px достаточно 1000-2000 точек данных.\n    *   **Алгоритм:** Разбить аудиобуфер на N сегментов (по числу пикселей по ширине графика). Для каждого сегмента рассчитать:\n        *   **RMS (Root Mean Square)** или **среднюю амплитуду** для \"основной\" формы волны.\n        *   **Пиковые значения (min/max)** для классического осциллографа.\n        *   **Спектральные данные (FFT)** для частотной визуализации. Для этого можно использовать `AnalyserNode` внутри `OfflineAudioContext`, продвигая время контекста.\n\n3.  **Кэширование результатов:**\n    *   Результаты предварительного анализа (массивы чисел для амплитуды, спектра и т.д.) должны сохраняться в памяти (например, в свойстве класса `AudioVisualizer`).\n    *   При изменении размеров канваса или параметров визуализации (масштаб, тип графика) пересчёт должен происходить из кэшированных данных, а не из исходного аудиобуфера.\n\n4.  **Быстрый рендеринг на Canvas:**\n    *   Функция отрисовки (`drawWaveform()`, `drawFrequency()`) должна работать **только с предварительно рассчитанным кэшем**, а не с `AnalyserNode` в реальном времени.\n    *   При скраббинге (перемещении ползунка) визуализация для видимой области перерисовывается моментально из кэша.\n\n5.  **Архитектурные изменения:**\n    *   **Режимы работы:** Чётко разделить логику на `mode: 'live'` (с микрофона, через `AnalyserNode` и `requestAnimationFrame`) и `mode: 'preview'` (для файлов, рендеринг из кэша).\n    *   **Интерфейс:** При загрузке файла — мгновенно запускать оффлайн-анализ и отрисовывать полную волновую форму на отдельном канвасе для навигации.\n    *   **Обратная связь:** Во время анализа большого файла показывать индикатор прогресса.\n\n**Критерии успеха (Acceptance Criteria):**\n1.  При загрузке аудиофайла формата WAV/MP3 его волновая форма (waveform) отображается на экране **в течение 1-3 секунд** (зависит от длины файла), **до нажатия кнопки Play**.\n2.  Окно приложения можно свернуть, развернуть — предварительно построенная визуализация остаётся на месте.\n3.  Перетаскивание ползунка прогресса (scrub) приводит к **мгновенной** перерисовке визуализации (осциллограф/спектр) для соответствующего момента времени.\n4.  Функциональность записи с микрофона и её \"живой\" визуализации **не сломана** и работает как прежде.\n5.  (Опционально) На больших файлах (>50 МБ) анализ запускается постепенно или с возможностью прервать.\n\n**Стек технологий для решения:**\n*   Web Audio API (`AudioContext`, `OfflineAudioContext`, `decodeAudioData`, `AudioBuffer`)\n*   Canvas API (`CanvasRenderingContext2D`)\n*   Возможна обработка в Web Worker для очень больших файлов, чтобы не блокировать основной поток.\n\n**Ссылки для вдохновения/изучения:**\n*   `OfflineAudioContext`: [MDN Documentation](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/OfflineAudioContext)\n*   `decodeAudioData`: [MDN Documentation](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/BaseAudioContext/decodeAudioData)\n*   Принцип работы waveform в Audacity или аудиоредакторах.","is_error":false}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"1a9f1585-6c98-4dd5-8774-2bf3e78ac97c","uuid":"6e469153-ed46-4c0c-8fc7-c05b85a70560","tool_use_result":{"stdout":"title:\tFix ofline rendering\nstate:\tOPEN\nauthor:\tJhon-Crow\nlabels:\t\ncomments:\t0\nassignees:\t\nprojects:\t\nmilestone:\t\nnumber:\t75\n--\n**Проблема (Текущее состояние):**\nТекущая система визуализации аудио (`AudioVisualizer`) работает исключительно в режиме реального времени, привязана к воспроизведению аудио через `HTMLAudioElement` и требует активного состояния окна/вкладки браузера (останавливается при сворачивании).     }\n    86→      this.canvas = element;\n    87→    } else {\n    88→      this.canvas = config.canvas;\n    89→    }\n    90→\n    91→    // Get 2D context with color space settings for better continues when tab is hidden or window is minimized\n   157→   */\n   158→  private handleVisibilityChange(): void {\n   159→    // Check if we have an active audio source that needs visualization\n   160→    if (this._sourceType === null) {\n   161→      return;\n   162→    }\n   163→\n   164→    if (document.hidden) {\n   165→      // Page is hidden, switch to timer-based animation\n   166→ interval (16ms) than the target frame rate because browsers may throttle timers\n   194→   * when the page is hidden, so we want to ensure frames are drawn as frequently as possible\n   195→   */\n   196→  private startTimerFallback(): void {\n   197→    if

406→\n   407→  /**\n   408→   * Show a brief demo visualization (for preview without audio source)\n   409→   * Useful for previewing visualization settings changes\n   410→   */\n   411→  showDemoVisualization(durationMs: number = 1000): void {\n   412→    // Stop any existing visualization\n   413→    this.stopVisualization();\n   414→\n   415→    let startTime: number | null =  613→    }\n   614→\n   615→    this.debugVisualActive = true;\n   616→    this.debugVisualStartTime = performance.now();\n   617→    this.log('Debug visual activated');\n   618→\n   619→    // Start 624→\n   625→      // Draw the debug visual boundaries\n   626→      this.drawDebugBoundaries(timestamp);\n   627→\n   628→      // Continue animation\n   629→      this.debugVisualAnimationId = 655→   */\n   656→  private drawDebugBoundaries(timestamp: number): void {\n   657→    const ctx = this.ctx;\n   658→    const width = this.canvas.width;\n   659→    const height = this.canvas.height;\n   660→\n   661→    // Calculate blink effect using sine wave for smooth pulsing\n   662→    // Period: 800ms for complete blink cycle\n   663→    const blinkPeriod = 800;\n   664→    const phase = ((timestamp - this.debugVisualStartTime) % blinkPeriod) / blinkPeriod;\n   665→    const opacity = 0.3 + 0.5 * Math.abs(Math.sin(phase * Math.PI * 2));\n   666→\n   667→    // Save current context state\n   668→    ctx.save();\n   669→\n   670→    // Draw outer boundary (main canvas boundary)\n   671→    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(255, 100, 100, ${opacity})`;\n   672→    ctx.lineWidth = 8;\n   673→    ctx.setLineDash([20, 10]);\n   674→    ctx.lineDashOffset = -(timestamp / 20);\n   675→    ctx.strokeRect(4, 4, width - 8, height - 8);\n   676→\n   677→    // Draw inner boundary (visualization area indicator)\n   678→    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(100, 200, 255, ${opacity * 0.7})`;\n   679→    ctx.lineWidth = 4;\n   680→    ctx.setLineDash([15, 8]);\n   681→    ctx.lineDashOffset = timestamp / 15;\n   682→    ctx.strokeRect(20, 20, width - 40, height - 40);\n   683→\n   684→    // Draw corner markers for better visibility\n   685→    const markerSize = 30;\n   686→    const markerColor = `rgba(255, 200, 50, ${opacity})`;\n   687→    ctx.strokeStyle = markerColor;\n   688→    ctx.lineWidth = 3;\n   689→    ctx.setLineDash([]);\n   690→\n   691→    // Top-left corner\n   692→    ctx.beginPath();\n   693→    ctx.moveTo(10, 10 + markerSize);\n   694→    ctx.lineTo(10, 10);\n   695→    ctx.lineTo(10 + markerSize, 10);\n   696→    ctx.stroke();\n   697→\n   698→    // Top-right corner\n   699→    ctx.beginPath();\n   700→    ctx.moveTo(width - 10 - markerSize, 10);\n   701→    ctx.lineTo(width - 10, 10);\n   702→    ctx.lineTo(width - 10, 10 + markerSize);\n   703→    ctx.stroke();\n   704→\n   705→    // Bottom-left corner\n   706→    ctx.beginPath();\n   707→    ctx.moveTo(10, height - 10 - markerSize);\n   708→    ctx.lineTo(10, height - 10);\n   709→    ctx.lineTo(10 + markerSize, height - 10);\n   710→    ctx.stroke();\n   711→\n   712→    // Bottom-right corner\n   713→    ctx.beginPath();\n   714→    ctx.moveTo(width - 10 - 217→  protected applySensitivity(value: number): number {\n   218→    const sensitivity = this.options.sensitivity ?? 1.0;\n   219→    return Math.min(255, value * sensitivity);\n   220→  }\n   221→\n     case 'color-flash':\n   307→        this.applyColorFlashEffect(ctx, width, height, phase, intensity);\n   308→        break;\n   309→    }\n   310→  }\n   311→\n   312→  /**\n   313→   * Gradient   319→    phase: number,\n   320→    intensity: number\n   321→  ): void {\n   322→    // Create an animated gradient that sweeps across the image\n   323→    // Phase 0->0.5: sweep in, 0.5->1: sweep out\n   324→    const sweepPhase = phase < 0.5 ? phase * 2 : (1 - phase) * 2;\n   325→    const alpha = sweepPhase * intensity * 0.6;\n   326→\n   327→    // Diagonal gradient sweep from top-left to bottom-right\n   328→    const gradientStart = (phase - 0.5) * (width + height);\n   329→    const gradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(\n   330→      gradientStart, gradientStart,\n   331→      gradientStart + width, gradientStart + height\n   332→    );\n   333→\n   334→    gradient.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0)');\n   335→    gradient.addColorStop(0.3, `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${alpha})`);\n   336→    gradient.addColorStop(0.7, `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${alpha})`);\n   337→    gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0)');\n   338→\n   339→    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'lighter';\n   340→    ctx.fillStyle = gradient;\n   341→    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);\n   342→    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';\n   343→  }\n   344→\n   345→  /**\n   346→   * Negative flash effect - invert colors briefly\n   347→   */\n   348→  private applyNegativeFlashEffect(\n   349→    ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D,\n   350→    _width: number,\n   351→    _height: number,\n   352→    phase: number,\n   353→    intensity: number\n   354→  ): void {\n   355→    // Quick flash effect: fade in and out\n   356→    const flashPhase = phase < 0.3 ? phase / 0.3 : (1 - phase) / 0.7;\n   357→    const effectStrength = flashPhase * intensity * 100;\n   358→\n   359→    // Apply invert filter\n   360→    ctx.filter = `invert(${effectStrength}%)`;\n   361→ applyBrightnessPulseEffect(\n   369→    ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D,\n   370→    _width: number,\n   371→    _height: number,\n   372→    phase: number,\n   373→    intensity: number\n   374→  ): data\n   787→   * @returns The smoothed value with ADSR envelope applied\n   788→   */\n   789→  protected applyADSRSmoothing(previousValue: number, targetValue: number): number {\n   790→    // Get ADSR parameters (0-100 scale)\n   791→    const attack = this.options.adsrAttack ?? 20;\n   792→    const decay = this.options.adsrDecay ?? 30;\n   793→    const sustain = this.options.adsrSustain ?? 10;\n   794→    const release = this.options.adsrRelease ?? 50;\n   795→\n   796→    // Calculate sustain floor based on target (higher target = higher sustain floor)\n   797→    const sustainFloor = targetValue * (sustain / 100);\n   798→\n   799→    // Determine if we're in attack (rising) or release (falling) phase\n   800→    if (targetValue > previousValue) {\n   801→      // Attack phase - value is rising toward target\n   802→      // Convert attack (0-100) to smoothing factor (0-1)\n   803→      // 0 = instant (no smoothing), 100 = very slow (high smoothing)\n   804→      const 808→      // Release/decay phase - value is falling\n   809→      // Apply sustain floor - don't let value fall below sustain level\n   810→      const effectiveTarget = Math.max(targetValue, sustainFloor);\n   811→\n   812→      // If we're above sustain level, use decay rate; if below, use release rate\n   813→      const isAboveSustain = previousValue > sustainFloor && targetValue >= sustainFloor * 0.5;\n   814→      const releaseSmoothing = isAboveSustain ? (decay / 100) : (release / 100);\n   815→\n   816→      const releasedValue = previousValue * releaseSmoothing + effectiveTarget * (1 - releaseSmoothing);\n   817→      return Math.max(releasedValue, sustainFloor);\n   818→    }\n   819→  }\n   820→\n   821→  /**\n   822→   * Clean up resources\n   823→   */\n   824→  destroy(): void {\n   825→    this.canvas = null;\n   826→    this.backgroundImageElement = null;\n   827→    this.foregroundImageElement = null;\n   828→    this.imageLoadPromises = [];\n   829→  }\n   830→}\n   831→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. }\n\n    // Calculate how many bins to use (from the start, as lower frequencies are more important)\n    // Ensure we have at least minBins bins to prevent division by zero issues\n    const effectiveMinBins = minBins ?? this.options.barCount ?? 1;\n    const calculatedBinCount = Math.floor((frequencyData.length * frequencyWidth) / 100);\n    const binCount = Math.max(effectiveMinBins, calculatedBinCount);\n\n    // Return a slice of the frequency data (capped at actual length)\n    return frequencyData.slice(0, Math.min(binCount, frequencyData.length));\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Calculate the average value for a frequency band with safe division\n   * @param frequencyData - Frequency data array\n   * @param startIndex - Start index in the array\n   * @param count - Number of bins to average (will be clamped to valid range)\n   * @returns Average value (0-255) or 0 if no valid data\n   */\n  protected calculateBandAverage(frequencyData: Uint8Array, startIndex: number, count: number): number {\n    if (count <= 0 || startIndex >= frequencyData.length) {\n      return 0;\n    }\n\n    // Clamp count to available data\n    const effectiveCount = Math.min(count, frequencyData.length - startIndex);\n    if (effectiveCount <= 0) {\n      return 0;\n    }\n\n    let sum = 0;\n    for (let i = 0; i < effectiveCount; i++) {\n      sum += frequencyData[startIndex + i];\n    }\n\n    return sum / effectiveCount;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Apply sensitivity multiplier to an audio data value\n   * @param value - The raw audio data value (typically 0-255)\n   * @returns The value multiplied by sensitivity and clamped to valid range (0-255)\n   */\n  protected applySensitivity(value: number): number {\n    const sensitivity = this.options.sensitivity ?? 1.0;\n    return Math.min(255, value * sensitivity);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Check if frequency-based blink should be triggered\n   * Analyzes frequency data in the specified range and checks against threshold\n   */\n  protected checkBlinkTrigger(data: VisualizationData): boolean {\n    if (!this.options.imageBlinkEnabled) {\n      return false;\n    }\n\n    const { frequencyData, sampleRate, fftSize } = data;\n    const frequencyRange = this.options.imageBlinkFrequencyRange!;\n    const threshold = this.options.imageBlinkVolumeThreshold!;\n\n    // Convert frequency range (Hz) to bin indices\n    // Each bin represents: sampleRate / fftSize Hz\n    const binSize = sampleRate / fftSize;\n    const minBin = Math.floor(frequencyRange.min / binSize);\n    const maxBin = Math.ceil(frequencyRange.max / binSize);\n\n    // Calculate average amplitude in the frequency range\n    let sum = 0;\n    let count = 0;\n    for (let i = minBin; i <= maxBin && i < frequencyData.length; i++) {\n      sum += frequencyData[i];\n      count++;\n    }\n\n    const average = count > 0 ? sum / count : 0;\n\n    // Trigger blink if average exceeds threshold\n    return average > threshold;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Update blink animation state based on trigger\n   */\n  protected updateBlinkState(triggered: boolean, timestamp: number): void {\n    const duration = this.options.imageBlinkDuration!;\n\n    if (triggered && !this.blinkActive) {\n      // Start new blink\n      this.blinkActive = true;\n      this.blinkStartTime = timestamp;\n      this.blinkAnimationPhase = 0;\n    }\n\n    if (this.blinkActive) {\n      // Update animation phase (0 to 1 over duration)\n      const elapsed = timestamp - this.blinkStartTime;\n      this.blinkAnimationPhase = Math.min(1, elapsed / duration);\n\n      // End blink when animation completes\n      if (this.blinkAnimationPhase >= 1) {\n        this.blinkActive = false;\n        this.blinkAnimationPhase = 0;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Apply image blink effect to a canvas\n   */\n  protected applyImageBlinkEffect(\n    ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D,\n    width: number,\n    height: number,\n    phase: number\n  ): void {\n    if (phase <= 0) return;\n\n    const style = this.options.imageBlinkStyle!;\n    const intensity = this.options.imageBlinkIntensity! / 100;\n\n    // Create effect overlay based on style\n    switch (style) {\n      case 'gradient-sweep':\n        this.applyGradientSweepEffect(ctx, width, height, phase, intensity);\n        break;\n      case 'negative-flash':\n        this.applyNegativeFlashEffect(ctx, width, height, phase, intensity);\n        break;\n      case 'brightness-pulse':\n        this.applyBrightnessPulseEffect(ctx, width, height, phase, intensity);\n        break;\n      case 'color-flash':\n        this.applyColorFlashEffect(ctx, width, height, phase, intensity);\n        break;\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Gradient sweep effect - animated gradient highlight\n   */\n  private applyGradientSweepEffect(\n    ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D,\n    width: number,\n    height: number,\n    phase: number,\n    intensity: number\n  ): void {\n    // Create an animated gradient that sweeps across the image\n    // Phase 0->0.5: sweep in, 0.5->1: sweep out\n    const sweepPhase = phase < 0.5 ? phase * 2 : (1 - phase) * 2;\n    const alpha = sweepPhase * intensity * 0.6;\n\n    // Diagonal gradient sweep from top-left to bottom-right\n    const gradientStart = (phase - 0.5) * (width + height);\n    const gradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(\n      gradientStart, gradientStart,\n      gradientStart + width, gradientStart + height\n    );\n\n    gradient.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0)');\n    gradient.addColorStop(0.3, `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${alpha})`);\n    gradient.addColorStop(0.7, `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${alpha})`);\n    gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0)');\n\n    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'lighter';\n    ctx.fillStyle = gradient;\n    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);\n    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Negative flash effect - invert colors briefly\n   */\n  private applyNegativeFlashEffect(\n    ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D,\n    _width: number,\n    _height: number,\n    phase: number,\n    intensity: number\n  ): void {\n    // Quick flash effect: fade in and out\n    const flashPhase = phase < 0.3 ? phase / 0.3 : (1 - phase) / 0.7;\n    const effectStrength = flashPhase * intensity * 100;\n\n    // Apply invert filter\n    ctx.filter = `invert(${effectStrength}%)`;\n    ctx.drawImage(ctx.canvas, 0, 0);\n    ctx.filter = 'none';\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Brightness pulse effect - brighten image\n   */\n  private applyBrightnessPulseEffect(\n    ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D,\n    _width: number,\n    _height: number,\n    phase: number,\n    intensity: number\n  ): void {\n    // Smooth pulse: fade in and out\n    const pulsePhase = phase < 0.5 ? phase * 2 : (1 - phase) * 2;\n    const brightness = 100 + pulsePhase * intensity * 100;\n\n    // Apply brightness filter\n    ctx.filter = `brightness(${brightness}%)`;\n    ctx.drawImage(ctx.canvas, 0, 0);\n    ctx.filter = 'none';\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Color flash effect - flash with primary color\n   */\n  private applyColorFlashEffect(\n    ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D,\n    width: number,\n    height: number,\n    phase: number,\n    intensity: number\n  ): void {\n    // Quick color flash: fade in and out\n    const flashPhase = phase < 0.3 ? phase / 0.3 : (1 - phase) / 0.7;\n    const alpha = flashPhase * intensity * 0.5;\n\n    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'lighter';\n    ctx.fillStyle = this.options.primaryColor!;\n    ctx.globalAlpha = alpha;\n    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);\n    ctx.globalAlpha = 1;\n    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Draw background (color or image) with optional blink effect\n   */\n  protected drawBackground(ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D, data: VisualizationData): void {\n    if (!this.options.drawBackground) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Check for blink trigger and update state\n    const shouldBlink = this.options.imageBlinkEnabled &&\n                        (this.options.imageBlinkTarget === 'background' || this.options.imageBlinkTarget === 'both');\n    if (shouldBlink) {\n      const triggered = this.checkBlinkTrigger(data);\n      this.updateBlinkState(triggered, data.timestamp);\n    }\n\n    if (this.backgroundImageElement) {\n      // Draw background image based on size mode\n      const mode = this.options.backgroundSizeMode || 'cover';\n      switch (mode) {\n        case 'cover':\n          this.drawImageCover(ctx, this.backgroundImageElement, data.width, data.height);\n          break;\n        case 'contain':\n          this.drawImageContain(ctx, this.backgroundImageElement, data.width, data.height);\n          break;\n        case 'stretch':\n          this.drawImageStretch(ctx, this.backgroundImageElement, data.width, data.height);\n          break;\n        case 'tile':\n          this.drawImageTile(ctx, this.backgroundImageElement, data.width, data.height);\n          break;\n        case 'center':\n          this.drawImageCenter(ctx, this.backgroundImageElement, data.width, data.height);\n          break;\n        case 'custom':\n          this.drawImageCustom(ctx, this.backgroundImageElement, data.width, data.height);\n          break;\n        default:\n          this.drawImageCover(ctx, this.backgroundImageElement, data.width, data.height);\n      }\n\n      // Apply blink effect to background if active\n      if (shouldBlink && this.blinkActive) {\n        this.applyImageBlinkEffect(ctx, data.width, data.height, this.blinkAnimationPhase);\n      }\n    } else {\n      ctx.fillStyle = this.options.backgroundColor!;\n      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, data.width, data.height);\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Apply layer effects to the background (between background and visualization)\n   * This should be called AFTER drawBackground to apply effect to background only\n   */\n  protected applyLayerEffect(ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D, data: VisualizationData): void {\n    const effect = this.options.layerEffect ?? 'none';\n    if (effect === 'none') {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const intensity = this.options.layerEffectIntensity ?? 50;\n    const { width, height } = data;\n\n    // Create a temporary canvas to capture current background\n    const tempCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');\n    tempCanvas.width = width;\n    tempCanvas.height = height;\n    const tempCtx = tempCanvas.getContext('2d');\n    if (!tempCtx) return;\n\n    // Copy current canvas content (background) to temp canvas\n    tempCtx.drawImage(ctx.canvas, 0, 0);\n\n    // Build the CSS filter value\n    let filterValue = '';\n    switch (effect) {\n      case 'blur':\n        filterValue = `blur(${(intensity / 100) * 10}px)`;\n        break;\n      case 'brightness':\n        filterValue = `brightness(${50 + (intensity / 100) * 150}%)`;\n        break;\n      case 'contrast':\n        filterValue = `contrast(${50 + (intensity / 100) * 150}%)`;\n        break;\n      case 'grayscale':\n        filterValue = `grayscale(${intensity}%)`;\n        break;\n      case 'invert':\n        filterValue = `invert(${intensity}%)`;\n        break;\n      case 'sepia':\n        filterValue = `sepia(${intensity}%)`;\n        break;\n      case 'saturate':\n        filterValue = `saturate(${intensity * 2}%)`;\n        break;\n      case 'hue-rotate':\n        filterValue = `hue-rotate(${(intensity / 100) * 360}deg)`;\n        break;\n    }\n\n    if (filterValue) {\n      // Clear the main canvas\n      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);\n      // Draw the background with the filter effect applied\n      ctx.filter = filterValue;\n      ctx.drawImage(tempCanvas, 0, 0);\n      ctx.filter = 'none';\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Draw foreground image if specified with optional blink effect\n   */\n  protected drawForeground(ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D, data: VisualizationData): void {\n    if (this.foregroundImageElement) {\n      const alpha = this.options.foregroundAlpha ?? 1;\n      const previousAlpha = ctx.globalAlpha;\n      ctx.globalAlpha = alpha;\n      this.drawImageCover(ctx, this.foregroundImageElement, data.width, data.height);\n      ctx.globalAlpha = previousAlpha;\n\n      // Apply blink effect to foreground if active and target includes foreground\n      const shouldBlink = this.options.imageBlinkEnabled &&\n                          (this.options.imageBlinkTarget === 'foreground' || this.options.imageBlinkTarget === 'both');\n      if (shouldBlink && this.blinkActive) {\n        this.applyImageBlinkEffect(ctx, data.width, data.height, this.blinkAnimationPhase);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Draw an image to cover the canvas (like CSS background-size: cover)\n   */\n  protected drawImageCover(\n    ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D,\n    img: HTMLImageElement,\n    width: number,\n    height: number\n  ): void {\n    const imgRatio = img.width / img.height;\n    const canvasRatio = width / height;\n\n    let drawWidth: number;\n    let drawHeight: number;\n    let offsetX: number;\n    let offsetY: number;\n\n    if (imgRatio > canvasRatio) {\n      // Image is wider than canvas\n      drawHeight = height;\n      drawWidth = height * imgRatio;\n      offsetX = (width - drawWidth) / 2;\n      offsetY = 0;\n    } else {\n      // Image is taller than canvas\n      drawWidth = width;\n      drawHeight = width / imgRatio;\n      offsetX = 0;\n      offsetY = (height - drawHeight) / 2;\n    }\n\n    ctx.drawImage(img, offsetX, offsetY, drawWidth, drawHeight);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Draw an image to fit within the canvas (like CSS background-size: contain)\n   */\n  protected drawImageContain(\n    ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D,\n    img: HTMLImageElement,\n    width: number,\n    height: number\n  ): void {\n    const imgRatio = img.width / img.height;\n    const canvasRatio = width / height;\n\n    let drawWidth: number;\n    let drawHeight: number;\n    let offsetX: number;\n    let offsetY: number;\n\n    if (imgRatio > canvasRatio) {\n      // Image is wider than canvas\n      drawWidth = width;\n      drawHeight = width / imgRatio;\n      offsetX = 0;\n      offsetY = (height - drawHeight) / 2;\n    } else {\n      // Image is taller than canvas\n      drawHeight = height;\n      drawWidth = height * imgRatio;\n      offsetX = (width - drawWidth) / 2;\n      offsetY = 0;\n    }\n\n    // Fill background first\n    ctx.fillStyle = this.options.backgroundColor!;\n    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);\n    ctx.drawImage(img, offsetX, offsetY, drawWidth, drawHeight);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Draw an image stretched to fill the canvas\n   */\n  protected drawImageStretch(\n    ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D,\n    img: HTMLImageElement,\n    width: number,\n    height: number\n  ): void {\n    ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, width, height);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Draw an image tiled across the canvas\n   */\n  protected drawImageTile(\n    ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D,\n    img: HTMLImageElement,\n    width: number,\n    height: number\n  ): void {\n    const pattern = ctx.createPattern(img, 'repeat');\n    if (pattern) {\n      ctx.fillStyle = pattern;\n      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Draw an image centered (actual size) on the canvas\n   */\n  protected visualization, and call restoreTransform() after\n   * When mirrorHorizontal is enabled, visualization diverges from center (left goes left, right goes right)\n   */\n  protected applyTransform(ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D, data?: { width: number; height: number }): void {\n    const offsetX = this.options.offsetX ?? 0;\n    const offsetY = this.options.offsetY ?? 0;\n    const scale = this.options.scale ?? 1;\n    const mirrorHorizontal = this.options.mirrorHorizontal ?? false;\n    const needsTransform = offsetX !== 0 || offsetY !== 0 || scale !== 1 || mirrorHorizontal;\n\n    if (needsTransform) {\n      ctx.save();\n      // If we have scale and dimensions, scale around center\n      if ((scale !== 1 || mirrorHorizontal) && data) {\n        const centerX = data.width / 2;\n drawn in restoreTransform\n        if (mirrorHorizontal) {\n          // Scale down to half width and shift to left quarter\n          ctx.scale(scale * 0.5, scale);\n          ctx.translate(-(centerX / 2) + offsetX / (scale * 0.5), -centerY + offsetY / scale);\n        } else {\n          ctx.scale(scale, scale);\n          ctx.translate(-centerX + offsetX / scale, -centerY + offsetY / scale);\n horizontal mirror is enabled\n   * Call this after drawing visualization if applyTransform() was called\n   * The mirror creates a diverging effect - visualization goes outward from center\n   */\n  protected restoreTransform(ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D, data?: { width: number; height: number }): void {\n    const offsetX = this.options.offsetX ?? 0;\n    const offsetY = this.options.offsetY ?? 0;\n    const scale = this.options.scale ?? 1;\n    const mirrorHorizontal = this.options.mirrorHorizontal ?? false;\n    const needsTransform = offsetX !== 0 || offsetY !== 0 || scale !== 1 || mirrorHorizontal;\n\n    if (needsTransform) {\n      ctx.restore();\n\n      // Draw horizontally mirrored copy - visualization diverges from center\n      // Left half shows normal visualization to scale -1)\n        ctx.drawImage(tempCanvas,\n          0, 0, centerX, height,  // Source: left half\n          centerX, 0, centerX, height  // Dest: right half (but flipped)\n        );\n /**\n   * Apply ADSR envelope smoothing to a value\n   * @param previousValue - The previous frame's value\n   * @param targetValue - The current target value from audio data\n   * @returns The smoothed value with ADSR envelope applied\n   */\n  protected applyADSRSmoothing(previousValue: number, targetValue: number): number {\n    // Get ADSR parameters (0-100 scale)\n    const attack = this.options.adsrAttack ?? 20;\n    const decay = this.options.adsrDecay ?? 30;\n    const sustain = this.options.adsrSustain ?? 10;\n    const release = this.options.adsrRelease ?? 50;\n\n    // Calculate sustain floor based on target (higher target = higher sustain floor)\n    const sustainFloor = targetValue * (sustain / 100);\n\n    // Determine if we're in attack (rising) or release (falling) phase\n    if (targetValue > previousValue) {\n      // Attack phase - value is rising toward target\n      // Convert attack (0-100) to smoothing factor (0-1)\n      // 0 = instant (no smoothing), 100 = very slow (high smoothing)\n      const attackSmoothing = attack / 100;\n      const attackedValue = previousValue * attackSmoothing + targetValue * (1 - attackSmoothing);\n      return attackedValue;\n    } else {\n      // Release/decay phase - value is falling\n      // Apply sustain floor - don't let value fall below sustain level\n      const effectiveTarget = Math.max(targetValue, sustainFloor);\n\n      // If we're above sustain level, use decay rate; if below, use release rate\n      const isAboveSustain = previousValue > sustainFloor && targetValue >= sustainFloor * 0.5;\n      const releaseSmoothing = isAboveSustain ? (decay / 100) : (release / 100);\n\n      const releasedValue = previousValue * releaseSmoothing + effectiveTarget * (1 - releaseSmoothing);\n      return Math.max(releasedValue, sustainFloor);\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Clean up resources\n   */\n  destroy(): void {\n    this.canvas = null;\n    this.backgroundImageElement = null;\n    this.foregroundImageElement = null;\n    this.imageLoadPromises = [];\n  }\n}\n",

          "content": "/**\n * Offline Audio Analyzer for pre-analyzing audio files\n * Provides fast waveform and frequency data without real-time playback\n *\n * This analyzer decodes audio files and pre-computes visualization data\n * that can be instantly accessed for any timestamp, enabling:\n * - Instant waveform preview before playback\n * - Smooth scrubbing through audio files\n * - Background analysis without blocking the UI\n * - Visualization that persists when window is minimized\n */\n\n/**\n * Cached visualization data for a single time point\n */\nexport interface Cache*************nData {\n  /** Time domain data (waveform) - values 0-255 */\n  timeDomainData: Uint8Array;\n  /** Frequency domain data (spectrum) - values 0-255 */\n  frequencyData: Uint8Array;\n  /** Peak amplitude for this segment (0-1) */\n  peakAmplitude: number;\n  /** RMS amplitude for this segment (0-1) */\n  rmsAmplitude: number;\n}\n\n/**\n * Full audio analysis cache containing all precomputed data\n */\nexport interface AudioAnalysisCache {\n  /** Duration of the audio in seconds */\n  duration: number;\n  /** Sample rate of the audio */\n  sampleRate: number;\n  /** Number of cached segments */\n  segmentCount: number;\n  /** Time interval between segments in seconds */\n  segmentDuration: number;\n  /** Cached data for each segment */\n  segments: CachedVisualizationData[];\n  /** The raw audio buffer (for advanced use cases) */\n  audioBuffer: AudioBuffer;\n  /** Number of data points per segment for time domain data */\n  fftSize: number;\n}\n\n/**\n * Progress callback for audio analysis\n */\nexport type Analy**************lback = (progress: number) => void;\n\n/**\n * Options for offline audio analysis\n */\nexport interface Offli************tions {\n  /** FFT size for frequency analysis (power of 2, 32-32768) */\n  fftSize?: number;\n  /** Target number of segments to cache (affects analysis granularity) */\n  targetSegments?: number;\n  /** Maximum segments to prevent memory issues with very long files */\n  maxSegments?: number;\n  /** Enable verbose logging */\n  debug?: boolean;\n}\n\n/**\n * Offline Audio Analyzer class\n * Pre-analyzes audio files for instant visualization access\n */\nexport class Offli**********lyzer {\n  private _fftSize: number;\n  private targetSegments: number;\n  private maxSegments: number;\n  private debug: boolean;\n  private cache: AudioAnalysisCache | null = null;\n  private analysisInProgress: boolean = false;\n  private abortController: AbortController | null = null;\n\n  constructor(options: Offli************tions = {}) {\n    this._fftSize = options.fftSize ?? 2048;\n    this.targetSegments = options.targetSegments ?? 1000;\n    this.maxSegments = options.maxSegments ?? 10000;\n    this.debug = options.debug ?? false;\n\n    // Validate FFT size\n    if (!this.isValidFftSize(this._fftSize)) {\n      throw new Error('FFT size must be a power of 2 between 32 and 32768');\n    }\n  }\n\n  private isValidFftSize(size: number): boolean {\n    return size >= 32 && size <= 32768 && (size & (size - 1)) === 0;\n  }\n\n  private log(...args: unknown[]): void {\n    if (this.debug) {\n      console.log('[OfflineAudioAnalyzer]', ...args);\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get FFT size\n   */\n  get fftSize(): number {\n    return this._fftSize;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Set FFT size (will require re-analysis)\n   */\n  set fftSize(value: number) {\n    if (!this.isValidFftSize(value)) {\n      throw new Error('FFT size must be a power of 2 between 32 and 32768');\n    }\n    this._fftSize = value;\n    // Invalidate cache when FFT size changes\n    this.cache = null;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Check if analysis is currently in progress\n   */\n  get isAnalyzing(): boolean {\n    return this.analysisInProgress;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get the current cache (if available)\n   */\n  get analysisCache(): AudioAnalysisCache | null {\n    return this.cache;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Check if audio has been analyzed and cached\n   */\n  get isCached(): boolean {\n    return this.cache !== null;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get the duration of the cached audio (or 0 if not cached)\n   */\n  get duration(): number {\n    return this.cache?.duration ?? 0;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Abort any in-progress analysis\n   */\n  abortAnalysis(): void {\n    if (this.abortController) {\n      this.abortController.abort();\n      this.abortController = null;\n    }\n    this.analysisInProgress = false;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Analyze an audio file and cache the visualization data\n   * @param source - File, URL string, or ArrayBuffer containing audio data\n   * @param onProgress - Optional progress callback (0-1)\n   * @returns Promise resolving to the analysis cache\n   */\n  async analyzeAudio(\n    source: File | string | ArrayBuffer,\n    onProgress?: AnalysisProgressCallback\n  ): Promise<AudioAnalysisCache> {\n    // Abort any previous analysis\n    this.abortAnalysis();\n\n    this.analysisInProgress = true;\n    this.abortController = new AbortController();\n    const signal = this.abortController.signal;\n\n    try {\n      this.log('Starting audio analysis...');\n\n      // Step 1: Load the audio data into an ArrayBuffer\n      let arrayBuffer: ArrayBuffer;\n      if (source instanceof ArrayBuffer) {\n        arrayBuffer = source;\n      } else if (source instanceof File) {\n        arrayBuffer = await source.arrayBuffer();\n      } else {\n        // URL string\n        const response = await fetch(source);\n        if (!response.ok) {\n          throw new Error(`Failed to fetch audio: ${response.statusText}`);\n        }\n        arrayBuffer = await response.arrayBuffer();\n      }\n\n      if (signal.aborted) {\n        throw new Error('Analysis aborted');\n      }\n\n      onProgress?.(0.1);\n      this.log('Audio data loaded, size:', arrayBuffer.byteLength, 'bytes');\n\n      // Step 2: Decode the audio using AudioContext\n      const audioContext = new AudioContext();\n      const audioBuffer = await audioContext.decodeAudioData(arrayBuffer.slice(0));\n      await audioContext.close();\n\n      if (signal.aborted) {\n        throw new Error('Analysis aborted');\n      }\n\n      onProgress?.(0.2);\n      this.log('Audio decoded:', {\n        duration: audioBuffer.duration,\n        sampleRate: audioBuffer.sampleRate,\n        channels: audioBuffer.numberOfChannels,\n        length: audioBuffer.length,\n      });\n\n      // Step 3: Calculate segment parameters\n      const duration = audioBuffer.duration;\n      const sampleRate = audioBuffer.sampleRate;\n\n      // Calculate optimal segment count (min 10, max maxSegments)\n      // For a typical 3-minute song at 1000 segments, each segment is ~180ms\n      let segmentCount = Math.min(\n        this.maxSegments,\n        Math.max(10, Math.min(this.targetSegments, Math.ceil(duration * 30))) // ~30 segments per second for smooth scrubbing\n      );\n\n      const segmentDuration = duration / segmentCount;\n      const samplesPerSegment = Math.floor(sampleRate * segmentDuration);\n\n      this.log('Analysis parameters:', {\n        segmentCount,\n        segmentDuration: segmentDuration.toFixed(3) + 's',\n        samplesPerSegment,\n      });\n\n      // Step 4: Pre-allocate result array\n      const segments: CachedVisualizationData[] = new Array(segmentCount);\n\n      // Step 5: Extract channel data (use channel 0, or mix stereo to mono)\n      let pcmData: Float32Array;\n      if (audioBuffer.numberOfChannels === 1) {\n        pcmData = audioBuffer.getChannelData(0);\n      } else {\n        // Mix stereo to mono\n        const left = audioBuffer.getChannelData(0);\n        const right = audioBuffer.getChannelData(1);\n        pcmData = new Float32Array(left.length);\n        for (let i = 0; i < left.length; i++) {\n          pcmData[i] = (left[i] + right[i]) / 2;\n        }\n      }\n\n      if (signal.aborted) {\n        throw new Error('Analysis aborted');\n      }\n\n      onProgress?.(0.3);\n\n      // Step 6: Analyze each segment\n      const frequencyBinCount = this._fftSize / 2;\n\n      for (let i = 0; i < segmentCount; i++) {\n        if (signal.aborted) {\n          throw new Error('Analysis aborted');\n        }\n\n        const startSample = Math.floor(i * samplesPerSegment);\n        const endSample = Math.min(startSample + samplesPerSegment, pcmData.length);\n\n        segments[i] = this.analyzeSegment(\n          pcmData,\n          startSample,\n          endSample,\n          this._fftSize,\n          frequencyBinCount,\n          sampleRate\n        );\n\n        // Report progress (20% for loading, 70% for analysis)\n        if (i % 50 === 0 || i === segmentCount - 1) {\n          const analysisProgress = 0.3 + (i / segmentCount) * 0.7;\n          onProgress?.(analysisProgress);\n        }\n      }\n\n      // Step 7: Create and store the cache\n      this.cache = {\n        duration,\n        sampleRate,\n        segmentCount,\n        segmentDuration,\n        segments,\n        audioBuffer,\n        fftSize: this._fftSize,\n      };\n\n      this.analysisInProgress = false;\n      onProgress?.(1);\n      this.log('Analysis complete:', this.cache.segmentCount, 'segments cached');\n\n      return this.cache;\n    } catch (error) {\n      this.analysisInProgress = false;\n      if ((error as Error).message !== 'Analysis aborted') {\n        this.log('Analysis failed:', error);\n      }\n      throw error;\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Analyze a single segment of audio data\n   */\n  private analyzeSegment(\n    pcmData: Float32Array,\n    startSample: number,\n    endSample: number,\n    fftSize: number,\n    frequencyBinCount: number,\n    sampleRate: number\n  ): Cache*************nData {\n    const segmentLength = endSample - startSample;\n\n    // Calculate peak and RMS amplitude\n    let peak = 0;\n    let sumSquares = 0;\n\n    for (let i = startSample; i < endSample; i++) {\n      const value = Math.abs(pcmData[i]);\n      peak = Math.max(peak, value);\n      sumSquares += pcmData[i] * pcmData[i];\n    }\n\n    const rms = Math.sqrt(sumSquares / segmentLength);\n\n    // Generate time domain data (downsampled waveform)\n    // Match the format of AnalyserNode.getByteTimeDomainData (0-255, 128 = center)\n    const timeDomainData = new Uint8Array(fftSize);\n    const step = Math.max(1, Math.floor(segmentLength / fftSize));\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < fftSize; i++) {\n      const sampleIndex = startSample + Math.min(i * step, segmentLength - 1);\n      // Convert from -1..1 to 0..255 range (128 is center/silence)\n      const value = pcmData[sampleIndex];\n      timeDomainData[i] = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, Math.round((value + 1) * 127.5)));\n    }\n\n    // Generate frequency data using simple DFT-like analysis\n    // This is a simplified frequency analysis that's fast but approximate\n    // For more accurate results, a proper FFT library could be used\n    const frequencyData = this.computeFrequencyData(\n      pcmData,\n      startSample,\n      endSample,\n      frequencyBinCount,\n      sampleRate\n    );\n\n    return {\n      timeDomainData,\n      frequencyData,\n      peakAmplitude: peak,\n      rmsAmplitude: rms,\n    };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Compute frequency data for a segment\n   * Uses a simplified magnitude spectrum approach\n   */\n  private computeFrequencyData(\n    pcmData: Float32Array,\n    startSample: number,\n    endSample: number,\n    frequencyBinCount: number,\n    _sampleRate: number\n  ): Uint8Array {\n    const frequencyData = new Uint8Array(frequencyBinCount);\n    const segmentLength = endSample - startSample;\n\n    // Use bands-based analysis for efficiency\n    // This approximates what you'd get from FFT but is much faster\n    const bandsPerOctave = 3;\n    const numBands = Math.min(frequencyBinCount, 64);\n\n    // Calculate energy in frequency bands using autocorrelation-like approach\n    // This is a simplified but fast method\n    for (let band = 0; band < numBands; band++) {\n      // Map band to approximate frequency range\n      // Lower bands = lower frequencies (longer periods)\n      const periodFactor = Math.pow(2, (numBands - band - 1) / bandsPerOctave);\n      const period = Math.max(2, Math.min(segmentLength / 2, Math.round(periodFactor * 4)));\n\n      let energy = 0;\n      let count = 0;\n\n      // Calculate energy at this approximate period\n      for (let i = startSample; i < endSample - period; i += period) {\n        const diff = Math.abs(pcmData[i] - pcmData[i + period]);\n        const product = pcmData[i] * pcmData[i + Math.floor(period / 2)];\n        energy += Math.abs(product) - diff * 0.5;\n        count++;\n      }\n\n      if (count > 0) {\n        energy = energy / count;\n      }\n\n      // Scale and clamp to 0-255 range\n      // Apply some boost to lower frequencies to match typical music visualization\n      const boost = 1 + (numBands - band) / numBands;\n      const scaledEnergy = Math.abs(energy) * 500 * boost;\n\n      // Map to the corresponding bins\n      const binStart = Math.floor((band / numBands) * frequencyBinCount);\n      const binEnd = Math.floor(((band + 1) / numBands) * frequencyBinCount);\n\n      for (let bin = binStart; bin < binEnd; bin++) {\n        frequencyData[bin] = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, Math.round(scaledEnergy)));\n      }\n    }\n\n    return frequencyData;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get visualization data for a specific time in the audio\n   * Returns cached data if available, or interpolates between segments\n   * @param time - Time in seconds\n   * @returns Cached visualization data for the specified time, or null if not cached\n   */\n  getDataAtTime(time: number): Cache*************nData | null {\n    if (!this.cache) {\n      return null;\n    }\n\n    // Clamp time to valid range\n    const clampedTime = Math.max(0, Math.min(time, this.cache.duration));\n\n    // Find the segment index\n    const segmentIndex = Math.floor(clampedTime / this.cache.segmentDuration);\n    const clampedIndex = Math.min(segmentIndex, this.cache.segmentCount - 1);\n\n    return this.cache.segments[clampedIndex];\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get visualization data for a time range (useful for waveform overview)\n   * @param startTime - Start time in seconds\n   * @param endTime - End time in seconds\n   * @param maxPoints - Maximum number of points to return\n   * @returns Array of cached visualization data\n   */\n  getDataInRange(\n    startTime: number,\n    endTime: number,\n    maxPoints: number = 100\n  ): CachedVisualizationData[] | null {\n    if (!this.cache) {\n      return null;\n    }\n\n    const startIndex = Math.floor(startTime / this.cache.segmentDuration);\n    const endIndex = Math.ceil(endTime / this.cache.segmentDuration);\n\n    const clampedStart = Math.max(0, startIndex);\n    const clampedEnd = Math.min(this.cache.segmentCount, endIndex);\n\n    const totalSegments = clampedEnd - clampedStart;\n    const step = Math.max(1, Math.floor(totalSegments / maxPoints));\n\n    const result: CachedVisualizationData[] = [];\n    for (let i = clampedStart; i < clampedEnd; i += step) {\n      result.push(this.cache.segments[i]);\n    }\n\n    return result;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get a waveform overview for the entire audio file\n   * Returns peak amplitudes suitable for drawing a waveform preview\n   * @param numPoints - Number of points to generate\n   * @returns Array of peak amplitude values (0-1)\n   */\n  getWaveformOverview(numPoints: number = 200): Float32Array | null {\n    if (!this.cache) {\n      return null;\n    }\n\n    const result = new Float32Array(numPoints);\n    const step = this.cache.segmentCount / numPoints;\n\n    for (let Step 2: Decode the audio using AudioContext\n      const audioContext = new AudioContext();\n      const audioBuffer = await audioContext.decodeAudioData(arrayBuffer.slice(0));\n      await This is a simplified but fast method\n    for (let band = 0; band < numBands; band++) {\n      // Map band to approximate frequency range\n      // Lower bands = lower frequencies (longer periods)\n period]);\n        const product = pcmData[i] * pcmData[i + Math.floor(period / 2)];\n        energy += Math.abs(product) - diff * 0.5;\n        count++;\n      }\n\n      if (count > 0) {\n        energy = energy / count;\n      }\n\n      // Scale and clamp to 0-255 range\n      // Apply some boost to lower frequencies to match typical music visualization\n      const boost = 1 + (numBands - band) / numBands;\n      const scaledEnergy = Math.abs(energy) * 500 * boost;\n\n      // Map to the corresponding bins\n      const binStart = Math.floor((band / numBands) * frequencyBinCount);\n Math.round(scaledEnergy)));\n      }\n    }\n\n    return frequencyData;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get visualization data for a specific time in the audio\n   * Returns cached data if available, or ParticleVisualizer,\n  'spectrum-gradient': SpectrumGradientVisualizer,\n  'glow-waveform': GlowWaveformVisualizer,\n  'vu-meter': VUMeterVisualizer,\n  spectrogram: SpectrogramVisualizer,\n  'spiral-waveform': SpiralWaveformVisualizer,\n  'radial-bars': RadialBarsVisualizer,\n  'frequency-rings': FrequencyRingsVisualizer,\n  'double-spiral': DoubleSpiralVisualizer,\n  pulse: PulseVisualizer,\n  'waterfall-bars': WaterfallBarsVisualizer,\n  grid: GridVisualizer,\n  lissajous: LissajousVisualizer,\n};\n\n/**\n * Main AudioRecorder class\n * Handles audio capture, visualization, and video recording\n */\nexport class AudioRecorder extends EventEmitter<AudioRecorderEvents> {\n  private canvas: HTMLCanvasElement;\n  private ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D;\n  private analyzer: AudioAnalyzer;\n  private videoRecorder: VideoRecorder;\n  private visualizer: Visualizer;\n  private animationFrameId: number | null = null;\n  private lastFrameTime = 0;\n  private frameInterval: number;\n  private micStream: MediaStream | null = null;\n  private audioElement: HTMLAudioElement | null = null;\n  private _sourceType: AudioSourceType | null = null;\n  private debug: boolean;\n  private _readyPromise: Promise<void>;\n  private timerIntervalId: ReturnType<typeof setInterval> | null = null;\n  private debugVisualActive = false;\n  private debugVisualAnimationId: number | null = null;\n  private debug**********tTime = 0;\n\n  // Offline preview mode properties\n  private offlineAnalyzer: Offli**********lyzer | null = null;\n  private previewMode: boolean = false;\n  private previewTime: number = 0;\n  private previewAudioElement: HTMLAudioElement | null = null;\n\n  constructor(config: AudioRecorderConfig) {\n    super();\n\n    // Get canvas element\n    if (typeof config.canvas === 'string') {\n      const element = document.querySelector(config.canvas);\n      if (!element || !(element instanceof HTMLCanvasElement)) {\n        throw new Error(`Canvas element not found: ${config.canvas}`);\n      }\n      this.canvas = element;\n    } else {\n      this.canvas = config.canvas;\n    }\n\n    // Get 2D context with color space settings for better color accuracy\n    const ctx = this.canvas.getContext('2d', {\n      alpha: true,\n      colorSpace: 'srgb',\n      willReadFrequently: false,\n    });\n    if (!ctx) {\n      throw new Error('Failed to get 2D context from canvas');\n    }\n    this.ctx = ctx;\n\n    // Set image smoothing for better quality\n    ctx.imageSmoothingEnabled = true;\n    ctx.imageSmoothingQuality = 'high';\n\n    this.debug = config.debug ?? false;\n\n    // Set canvas size\n    if (config.videoWidth) {\n      this.canvas.width = config.videoWidth;\n    }\n    if (config.videoHeight) {\n      this.canvas.height = config.videoHeight;\n    }\n\n    // Initialize audio analyzer\n    this.analyzer = new AudioAnalyzer({\n      fftSize: config.fftSize ?? 2048,\n      smoothingTimeConstant: config.smoothingTimeConstant ?? 0.8,\n      debug: this.debug,\n    });\n\n    // Initialize video recorder\n    this.videoRecorder = new VideoRecorder({ debug: this.debug });\n\n    // Calculate frame interval for target FPS\n    const fps = config.fps ?? 30;\n    this.frameInterval = 1000 / fps;\n\n    // Initialize visualizer\n    if (config.visualizer) {\n      if (typeof config.visualizer === 'string') {\n        this.visualizer = this.createBuiltInVisualizer(\n          config.visualizer,\n          config.visualizerOptions\n        );\n      } else {\n        this.visualizer = config.visualizer;\n      }\n    } else {\n      this.visualizer = new BarVisualizer(config.visualizerOptions);\n    }\n\n    // Initialize visualizer and store the ready promise\n    const initResult = this.visualizer.init(this.canvas, config.visualizerOptions);\n    this._readyPromise = initResult instanceof Promise ? initResult : Promise.resolve();\n\n    // Set up visibility change handler for tab switching\n    this.handleVisibilityChange = this.handleVisibilityChange.bind(this);\n    document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', this.handleVisibilityChange);\n\n    this.log('AudioRecorder initialized');\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Handle page visibility changes to ensure visualization continues when tab is hidden or window is minimized\n   */\n  private handleVisibilityChange(): void {\n    // Check if we have an active audio source that needs visualization\n    if (this._sourceType === null) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    if (document.hidden) {\n      // Page is hidden, switch to timer-based animation\n      this.log('Page hidden, switching to timer-based visualization');\n\n      // Stop requestAnimationFrame\n      if (this.animationFrameId !== null) {\n        cancelAnimationFrame(this.animationFrameId);\n        this.animationFrameId = null;\n      }\n\n      // Start timer-based animation\n      this.startTimerFallback();\n    } else {\n      // Page is visible again, switch back to requestAnimationFrame\n      this.log('Page visible, switching to requestAnimationFrame');\n\n      // Stop timer\n      this.stopTimerFallback();\n\n      // Restart reque***********Frame if we have an active source\n      if (this._sourceType !== null) {\n        this.startVisualization();\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Start timer-based fallback for visualization when tab is hidden or window is minimized\n   * Note: setInterval is used instead of reque***********Frame because rAF pauses when tab/window is not visible\n   * We use a shorter interval (16ms) than the target frame rate because browsers may throttle timers\n   * when the page is hidden, so we want to ensure frames are drawn as frequently as possible\n   */\n  private startTimerFallback(): void {\n    if (this.timerIntervalId !== null) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Use a shorter polling interval (16ms ~ 60fps) to ensure frames are drawn\n    // even when the browser throttles the timer. The actual frame rate is still\n    // controlled by lastFrameTime check.\n    const pollingInterval = Math.min(16, this.frameInterval);\n\n    this.timerIntervalId = setInterval(() => {\n      const timestamp = performance.now();\n      if (timestamp - this.lastFrameTime >= this.frameInterval) {\n        this.lastFrameTime = timestamp;\n        this.drawFrame(timestamp);\n      }\n    }, pollingInterval);\n\n    this.log('Started timer fallback visualization with polling interval:', pollingInterval);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Stop timer-based fallback\n   */\n  private stopTimerFallback(): void {\n    if (this.timerIntervalId !== null) {\n      clearInterval(this.timerIntervalId);\n      this.timerIntervalId = null;\n      this.log('Stopped timer fallback visualization');\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Wait for the AudioRecorder to be fully ready (including image loading)\n   * Call this before starting visualization if using background/foreground images\n   */\n  async ready(): Promise<void> {\n    return this._readyPromise;\n  }\n\n  private log(...args: unknown[]): void {\n    if (this.debug) {\n      console.log('[AudioRecorder]', ...args);\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Create a built-in visualizer by name\n   */\n  private createBuiltInVisualizer(\n    name: string,\n    options?: VisualizerOptions\n  ): Visualizer {\n    const VisualizerClass = BUILT_IN_VISUALIZERS[name];\n    if (!VisualizerClass) {\n      throw new Error(\n        `Unknown visualizer: ${name}. Available: ${Object.keys(BUILT_IN_VISUALIZERS).join(', ')}`\n      );\n    }\n    return new VisualizerClass(options);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Start capturing audio from microphone\n   */\n  async startMicrophone(): Promise<void> {\n    try {\n      this.micStream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({\n        audio: {\n          echoCancellation: false,\n          noiseSuppression: false,\n          autoGainControl: false,\n        },\n      });\n\n      await this.analyzer.connectStream(this.micStream);\n      this._sourceType = 'microphone';\n      this.emit('source:change', 'microphone');\n      this.startVisualization();\n      this.log('Started microphone capture');\n    } catch (error) {\n      this.emit('error', error instanceof Error ? error : new Error(String(error)));\n      throw error;\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Connect an audio file for visualization\n   */\n  async connectAudioFile(file: File | string): Promise<HTMLAudioElement> {\n    try {\n      this.stopMicrophone();\n\n      // Create audio element\n      this.audioElement = new Audio();\n      this.audioElement.crossOrigin = 'anonymous';\n\n      if (file instanceof File) {\n        this.audioElement.src = URL.createObjectURL(file);\n      } else {\n        this.audioElement.src = file;\n      }\n\n      await this.analyzer.connectAudioElement(this.audioElement);\n      this._sourceType = 'file';\n      this.emit('source:change', 'file');\n      this.startVisualization();\n      this.log('Connected audio file');\n\n      return this.audioElement;\n    } catch (error) {\n      this.emit('error', error instanceof Error ? error : new Error(String(error)));\n      throw error;\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Stop microphone capture\n   */\n  stopMicrophone(): void {\n    if (this.micStream) {\n      this.micStream.getTracks().forEach((track) => track.stop());\n      this.micStream = null;\n      this.log('Stopped microphone');\n    }\n    this.analyzer.disconnect();\n    this._sourceType = null;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Start visualization loop\n   */\n  private startVisualization(): void {\n    if (this.animationFrameId !== null) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const animate = (timestamp: number): void => {\n      // Limit frame rate\n      if (timestamp - this.lastFrameTime >= this.frameInterval) {\n        this.lastFrameTime = timestamp;\n        this.drawFrame(timestamp);\n      }\n\n      this.animationFrameId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n    };\n\n    this.animationFrameId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n    this.log('Started visualization');\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Stop visualization loop\n   */\n  stopVisualization(): void {\n    if (this.animationFrameId !== null) {\n      cancelAnimationFrame(this.animationFrameId);\n      this.animationFrameId = null;\n    }\n    // Also stop timer fallback if active\n    this.stopTimerFallback();\n    this.log('Stopped visualization');\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Resume visualization loop\n   * Use this to restart visualization after it was stopped (e.g., during audio-to-video conversion)\n   * Only works if an audio source is connected\n   */\n  resumeVisualization(): void {\n    if (this._sourceType !== null) {\n      this.startVisualization();\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Draw a single visualization frame\n   */\n  private drawFrame(timestamp: number): void {\n    const data: VisualizationData = {\n      timeDomainData: this.analyzer.getTimeDomainData(),\n      frequencyData: this.analyzer.getFrequencyData(),\n      timestamp,\n      width: this.canvas.width,\n      height: this.canvas.height,\n      sampleRate: this.analyzer.sampleRate,\n      fftSize: this.analyzer.fftSize,\n    };\n\n    this.visualizer.draw(this.ctx, data);\n    this.emit('frame', data);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Draw a single demo frame (for preview without audio source)\n   */\n  private drawDemoFrame(timestamp: number): void {\n    const data: VisualizationData = {\n      timeDomainData: this.analyzer.generateDemoTimeDomainData(),\n      frequencyData: this.analyzer.generateDemoFrequencyData(),\n      timestamp,\n      width: this.canvas.width,\n      height: this.canvas.height,\n      sampleRate: this.analyzer.sampleRate,\n      fftSize: this.analyzer.fftSize,\n    };\n\n    this.visualizer.draw(this.ctx, data);\n    this.emit('frame', data);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Show a brief demo visualization (for preview without audio source)\n   * Useful for previewing visualization settings changes\n   */\n  showDemoVisualization(durationMs: number = 1000): void {\n    // Stop any existing visualization\n    this.stopVisualization();\n\n    let startTime: number | null = null;\n    const animate = (timestamp: number): void => {\n      if (startTime === null) {\n        startTime = timestamp;\n      }\n\n      const elapsed = timestamp - startTime;\n\n      // Limit frame rate\n      if (timestamp - this.lastFrameTime >= this.frameInterval) {\n        this.lastFrameTime = timestamp;\n        this.drawDemoFrame(timestamp);\n      }\n\n      // Continue animation if duration hasn't elapsed\n      if (elapsed < durationMs) {\n        this.animationFrameId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n      } else {\n        // Clean up after demo\n        this.animationFrameId = null;\n        // If there was an active source, restart its visualization\n        if (this._sourceType !== null) {\n          this.startVisualization();\n        }\n      }\n    };\n\n    this.animationFrameId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n    this.log('Started demo visualization for', durationMs, 'ms');\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Analyze an audio file for offline preview mode\n   * This pre-computes visualization data for the entire file, enabling:\n   * - Instant waveform preview before playback\n   * - Smooth scrubbing through the audio\n   * - Visualization that persists when window is minimized\n   *\n   * @param source - File, URL string, or ArrayBuffer containing audio data\n   * @param onProgress - Optional progress callback (0-1)\n   * @returns Promise resolving to the analysis cache\n   */\n  async analyzeAudioFile(\n    source: File | string | ArrayBuffer,\n    onProgress?: AnalysisProgressCallback\n  ): Promise<AudioAnalysisCache> {\n    // Create offline analyzer if not exists\n    if (!this.offlineAnalyzer) {\n      this.offlineAnalyzer = new OfflineAudioAnalyzer({\n        fftSize: this.analyzer.fftSize,\n        debug: this.debug,\n      });\n    }\n\n    this.log('Starting offline audio analysis...');\n    const cache = await this.offlineAnalyzer.analyzeAudio(source, onProgress);\n    this.log('Audio analysis complete:', cache.segmentCount, 'segments');\n\n    return cache;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Connect an audio file with offline preview support\n   * This will analyze the audio file first, then set up playback\n   * The waveform will be visible immediately after analysis, before pressing Play\n   *\n   * @param file - File or URL string for the audio\n   * @param onAnalysisProgress - Optional progress callback for analysis phase (0-1)\n   * @returns Promise resolving to the HTMLAudioElement for playback control\n   */\n  async connectAudioFileWithPreview(\n    file: File | string,\n    onAnalysisProgress?: AnalysisProgressCallback\n  ): Promise<HTMLAudioElement> {\n    try {\n      this.stopMicrophone();\n      this.stopPreview();\n\n      // First, analyze the audio file offline\n      await this.analyzeAudioFile(file, onAnalysisProgress);\n\n      // Create audio element for playback\n      this.previewAudioElement = new Audio();\n      this.previewAudioElement.crossOrigin = 'anonymous';\n\n      if (file instanceof File) {\n        this.previewAudioElement.src = URL.createObjectURL(file);\n      } else {\n        this.previewAudioElement.src = file;\n      }\n\n      // Wait for audio element to be ready\n      await new Promise<void>((resolve, reject) => {\n        if (this.previewAudioElement) {\n          this.previewAudioElement.onloadedmetadata = () => resolve();\n          this.previewAudioElement.onerror = () => reject(new Error('Failed to load audio'));\n        } else {\n          reject(new Error('Audio element not created'));\n        }\n      });\n\n      // Enable preview mode and show initial visualization\n      this.previewMode = true;\n      this.previewTime = 0;\n      this._sourceType = 'file';\n\n      // Set up audio element event handlers for synchronized visualization\n      this.previewAudioElement.ontimeupdate = () => {\n        if (this.previewAudioElement && this.previewMode) {\n          this.previewTime = this.previewAudioElement.currentTime;\n        }\n      };\n\n      // Start preview visualization\n      this.startPreviewVisualization();\n\n      this.emit('source:change', 'file');\n      this.log('Connected audio file with preview mode');\n\n      return this.previewAudioElement;\n    } catch (error) {\n      this.emit('error', error instanceof Error ? error : new Error(String(error)));\n      throw error;\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Start visualization in preview mode using cached offline data\n   */\n  private startPreviewVisualization(): void {\n    if (this.animationFrameId !== null) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const animate = (timestamp: number): void => {\n      // Limit frame rate\n      if (timestamp - this.lastFrameTime >= this.frameInterval) {\n        this.lastFrameTime = timestamp;\n        this.drawPreviewFrame(timestamp);\n      }\n\n      this.animationFrameId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n    };\n\n    this.animationFrameId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n    this.log('Started preview visualization');\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Draw a frame using cached offline data\n   */\n  private drawPreviewFrame(timestamp: number): void {\n    if (!this.offlineAnalyzer || !this.offlineAnalyzer.isCached) {\n      // Fallback to demo data if cache not available\n      this.drawDemoFrame(timestamp);\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Get cached data for current preview time\n    const cachedData = this.offlineAnalyzer.getDataAtTime(this.previewTime);\n    if (!cachedData) {\n      this.drawDemoFrame(timestamp);\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const cache = this.offlineAnalyzer.analysisCache!;\n\n    const data: VisualizationData = {\n      timeDomainData: cachedData.timeDomainData,\n      frequencyData: cachedData.frequencyData,\n      timestamp,\n      width: this.canvas.width,\n      height: this.canvas.height,\n      sampleRate: cache.sampleRate,\n      fftSize: cache.fftSize,\n    };\n\n    this.visualizer.draw(this.ctx, data);\n    this.emit('frame', data);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Seek to a specific time in preview mode\n   * This will instantly update the visualization to show the waveform at that time\n   *\n   * @param time - Time in seconds to seek to\n   */\n  seekPreview(time: number): void {\n    if (!this.previewMode || !this.offlineAnalyzer?.isCached) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const duration = this.offlineAnalyzer.duration;\n    this.previewTime = Math.max(0, Math.min(time, duration));\n\n    // Also seek the audio element if it exists\n    if (this.previewAudioElement) {\n      this.previewAudioElement.currentTime = this.previewTime;\n    }\n\n    // Force an immediate redraw\n    this.drawPreviewFrame(performance.now());\n\n    this.log('Seeked preview to:', this.previewTime.toFixed(2), 'seconds');\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get the waveform overview for the analyzed audio\n   * Returns peak amplitudes suitable for drawing a waveform preview/scrubber\n   *\n   * @param numPoints - Number of points to generate (default: 200)\n   * @returns Array of peak amplitude values (0-1), or null if no audio is analyzed\n   */\n  getWaveformOverview(numPoints: number = 200): Float32Array | null {\n    return this.offlineAnalyzer?.getWaveformOverview(numPoints) ?? null;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get the duration of the analyzed audio\n   * @returns Duration in seconds, or 0 if no audio is analyzed\n   */\n  getPreviewDuration(): number {\n    return this.offlineAnalyzer?.duration ?? 0;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get the current preview time\n   * @returns Current time in seconds\n   */\n  getPreviewTime(): number {\n    return this.previewTime;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Check if preview mode is active\n   */\n  get isPreviewMode(): boolean {\n    return this.previewMode;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Check if offline analysis is in progress\n   */\n  get isAnalyzing(): boolean {\n    return this.offlineAnalyzer?.isAnalyzing ?? false;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Check if audio has been analyzed and cached\n   */\n  get hasAnalysisCache(): boolean {\n    return this.offlineAnalyzer?.isCached ?? false;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get the audio element used for preview playback\n   */\n  getPreviewAudioElement(): HTMLAudioElement | null {\n    return this.previewAudioElement;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Play the preview audio\n   * Visualization will sync with playback automatically\n   */\n  async playPreview(): Promise<void> {\n    if (this.previewAudioElement) {\n      await this.previewAudioElement.play();\n      this.log('Started preview playback');\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Pause the preview audio\n   */\n  pausePreview(): void {\n    if (this.previewAudioElement) {\n      this.previewAudioElement.pause();\n      this.log('Paused preview playback');\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Stop preview mode and clean up resources\n   */\n  stopPreview(): void {\n    this.stopVisualization();\n    this.previewMode = false;\n    this.previewTime = 0;\n\n    if (this.previewAudioElement) {\n      this.previewAudioElement.pause();\n      if (this.previewAudioElement.src.startsWith('blob:')) {\n        URL.revokeObjectURL(this.previewAudioElement.src);\n      }\n      this.previewAudioElement = null;\n    }\n\n    this.log('Stopped preview mode');\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Abort any in-progress offline analysis\n   */\n  abortAnalysis(): void {\n    this.offlineAnalyzer?.abortAnalysis();\n    this.log('Aborted offline analysis');\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Start recording video\n   */\n  startRecording(options?: {\n    videoBitrate?: number;\n    audioBitrate?: number;\n  }): void {\n    if (this.videoRecorder.state !== 'inactive') {\n      throw new Error('Recording already in progress');\n    }\n\n    this.videoRecorder.start(this.canvas, this.micStream ?? undefined, {\n      fps: 1000 / this.frameInterval,\n      ...options,\n    });\n\n    this.emit('recording:start', undefined);\n    this.log('Started recording');\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Pause recording\n   */\n  pauseRecording(): void {\n    this.videoRecorder.pause();\n    this.emit('recording:pause', undefined);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Resume recording\n   */\n  resumeRecording(): void {\n    this.videoRecorder.resume();\n    this.emit('recording:resume', undefined);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Stop recording and return the video blob\n   */\n  async stopRecording(): Promise<Blob> {\n    const blob = await this.videoRecorder.stop();\n    this.emit('recording:stop', blob);\n    this.log('Stopped recording, blob size:', blob.size);\n    return blob;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Cancel recording and discard data\n   */\n  cancelRecording(): void {\n    this.videoRecorder.cancel();\n    this.log('Cancelled recording');\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Change visualizer\n   * @returns Promise that resolves when the new visualizer is fully initialized\n   */\n  async setVisualizer(visualizer: Visualizer | string, options?: VisualizerOptions): Promise<void> {\n    this.visualizer.destroy();\n\n    if (typeof visualizer === 'string') {\n      this.visualizer = this.createBuiltInVisualizer(visualizer, options);\n    } else {\n      this.visualizer = visualizer;\n    }\n\n    // Wait for visualizer initialization (including image loading) to prevent flickering\n    const initResult = this.visualizer.init(this.canvas, options);\n    this._readyPromise = initResult instanceof Promise ? initResult : Promise.resolve();\n    await this._readyPromise;\n    this.emit('visualizer:change', this.visualizer);\n    this.log('Changed visualizer to:', this.visualizer.name);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Update visualizer options\n   * @returns Promise that resolves when any image loading is complete\n   */\n  async setVisualizerOptions(options: Partial<VisualizerOptions>): Promise<void> {\n    if (this.visualizer.setOptions) {\n      const result = this.visualizer.setOptions(options);\n      if (result instanceof Promise) {\n        await result;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get current visualizer\n   */\n  getVisualizer(): Visualizer {\n    return this.visualizer;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get list of available built-in visualizers\n   */\n  static getAvailableVisualizers(): string[] {\n    return Object.keys(BUILT_IN_VISUALIZERS);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get recording state\n   */\n  get recordingState(): RecordingState {\n    return this.videoRecorder.state;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get current audio source type\n   */\n  get sourceType(): AudioSourceType | null {\n    return this._sourceType;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Check if visualization is active\n   */\n  get isVisualizationActive(): boolean {\n    return this.animationFrameId !== null || this.timerIntervalId !== null;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get canvas element\n   */\n  getCanvas(): HTMLCanvasElement {\n    return this.canvas;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get current frequency data (spectrum) for external use (e.g., presentation mode)\n   * Returns empty data if no audio source is active\n   */\n  getFrequencyData(): Uint8Array | null {\n    return this.analyzer.getFrequencyData();\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get current time domain data (waveform) for external use (e.g., presentation mode)\n   * Returns empty data if no audio source is active\n   */\n  getTimeDomainData(): Uint8Array | null {\n    return this.analyzer.getTimeDomainData();\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get audio context\n   */\n  getAudioContext(): AudioContext {\n    return this.analyzer.getAudioContext();\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get supported recording formats\n   */\n  static getSupportedFormats(): string[] {\n    return VideoRecorder.getSupportedFormats();\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Show debug visual boundaries with blink effect\n   * Displays a blinking boundary around the canvas to indicate active parameter changes\n   */\n  showDebugVisual(): void {\n    if (this.debugVisualActive) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    this.debugVisualActive = true;\n    this.debugVisualStartTime = performance.now();\n    this.log('Debug visual activated');\n\n    // Start the animation loop for the debug visual\n    const animateDebugVisual = (timestamp: number): void => {\n      if (!this.debugVisualActive) {\n        return;\n      }\n\n      // Draw the debug visual boundaries\n      this.drawDebugBoundaries(timestamp);\n\n      // Continue animation\n      this.debugVisualAnimationId = requestAnimationFrame(animateDebugVisual);\n    };\n\n    this.debugVisualAnimationId = requestAnimationFrame(animateDebugVisual);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Hide debug visual boundaries\n   */\n  hideDebugVisual(): void {\n    if (!this.debugVisualActive) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    this.debugVisualActive = false;\n\n    if (this.debugVisualAnimationId !== null) {\n      cancelAnimationFrame(this.debugVisualAnimationId);\n      this.debugVisualAnimationId = null;\n    }\n\n    this.log('Debug visual deactivated');\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Draw debug boundaries with blink effect\n   */\n  private drawDebugBoundaries(timestamp: number): void {\n    const ctx = this.ctx;\n    const width = this.canvas.width;\n    const height = this.canvas.height;\n\n    // Calculate blink effect using sine wave for smooth pulsing\n    // Period: 800ms for complete blink <li><strong>Instant Preview:</strong> Waveform and visualization appear immediately after analysis</li>\n        <li><strong>Smooth Scrubbing:</strong> Click anywhere on the waveform to seek - visualization updates instantly</li>\n        <li><strong>Background Resilient:</strong> Visualization works even when tab is minimized</li>\n        <li><strong>Progress Tracking:</strong> Analysis progress is reported in real-time</li>\n      </ul>\n    </div>\n  </div>\n\n  <script type=\"module\">\n    import { AudioRecorder } from '../dist/index.esm.js';\n\n    // Get DOM elements\n    const const playButton = document.getElementById('playButton');\n    const pauseButton = document.getElementById('pauseButton');\n    const canvas = document.getElementById('visualizerCanvas');\n    const document.getElementById('waveformProgress');\n    const waveformIndicator = document.getElementById('waveformIndicator');\n    const timeDisplay = document.getElementById('timeDisplay');\n    const
